Thursday, Septembsr 12, 1311

Mrs. GIBBS is unfortunate in being obliged to
inform the Publick, that the serious indispusition of
Mr. FA W C E T T renders it impossible for him to appear in those Characters for which he hcs been announced, in the Entertainments of this Evening.
Under the circumstances of this lamented aecident,
Mr. MALLINSON has obligingly consented to resume
the part of Acres in the Play, and Mr. F A R L E Y (by
permission of the Proprietors of the Theatre-Royal,
^Covent-Garden) has, upoa the shortest Rotice, undertaken to perform the character of Scout, in the Farce.
—-Mrs. Gibbs i a treats the liberal indulgence of the
Publick on this occasion.

of evincing her gratitude for that patronage with which she has been, asnua!h\ honou. r "*Through the liberality of the Proprietors of Covent Garden Theatre—and through the'
friendship of Performers, who are advertised under the permission of the above Proprietors,r--(.n addition to the present Company in the Hay Market) She respectfully trusts
that the establtshM .Favourites, thus concentrated, will produce a combination of taledt

the first representation of MY LANDLADY'S GOWN on Saturday last. It
will be acted every evening this week.

BY MISTAKE, it will be repeated TO-MORROW, and on Wednesday, and Saturday next
